import org.junit.jupiter.engine.extension.ExtensionRegistry;
import org.junit.platform.commons.JUnitException;
import org.junit.platform.commons.logging.Logger;
import org.junit.platform.commons.logging.LoggerFactory;
import org.junit.platform.commons.util.Preconditions;
import org.junit.platform.commons.util.UnrecoverableExceptions;
import org.junit.platform.engine.EngineExecutionListener;
import org.junit.platform.engine.TestDescriptor;
import org.junit.platform.engine.TestTag;
import org.junit.platform.engine.reporting.FileEntry;
import org.junit.platform.engine.reporting.ReportEntry;
import org.junit.platform.engine.support.hierarchical.Node;
import org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.NamespacedHierarchicalStore;

/**
 * @since 5.0
 */
abstract class AbstractExtensionContext<T extends TestDescriptor> implements ExtensionContextInternal, AutoCloseable {

	private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AbstractExtensionContext.class);

	private final @Nullable ExtensionContext parent;
	private final EngineExecutionListener engineExecutionListener;
	private final T testDescriptor;
	private final Set<String> tags;
	private final JupiterConfiguration configuration;
	private final ExecutableInvoker executableInvoker;
	private final ExtensionRegistry extensionRegistry;
	private final LauncherStoreFacade launcherStoreFacade;
	private final NamespacedHierarchicalStore<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> valuesStore;

	AbstractExtensionContext(@Nullable ExtensionContext parent, EngineExecutionListener engineExecutionListener,
			T testDescriptor, JupiterConfiguration configuration, ExtensionRegistry extensionRegistry,
			LauncherStoreFacade launcherStoreFacade) {

		Preconditions.notNull(testDescriptor, "TestDescriptor must not be null");
		Preconditions.notNull(configuration, "JupiterConfiguration must not be null");
		Preconditions.notNull(extensionRegistry, "ExtensionRegistry must not be null");
		this.executableInvoker = new DefaultExecutableInvoker(this, extensionRegistry);
		this.parent = parent;
		this.engineExecutionListener = engineExecutionListener;
		this.testDescriptor = testDescriptor;
		this.configuration = configuration;
		this.extensionRegistry = extensionRegistry;
		this.launcherStoreFacade = launcherStoreFacade;

		// @formatter:off
		this.tags = testDescriptor.getTags().stream()
				.map(TestTag::getName)
				.collect(collectingAndThen(toCollection(LinkedHashSet::new), Collections::unmodifiableSet));
		// @formatter:on

		this.valuesStore = createStore(parent, launcherStoreFacade, createCloseAction());
	}

	@SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
	private NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> createCloseAction() {
		return (__, ___, value) -> {
			boolean isAutoCloseEnabled = this.configuration.isClosingStoredAutoCloseablesEnabled();

			if (value instanceof @SuppressWarnings("resource") AutoCloseable closeable && isAutoCloseEnabled) {
				closeable.close();
				return;
			}

			if (value instanceof Store.CloseableResource resource) {
				if (isAutoCloseEnabled) {
					LOGGER.warn(
						() -> "Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: " + value.getClass().getName());
				}
				resource.close();
			}
		};
	}

	private static NamespacedHierarchicalStore<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> createStore(
			@Nullable ExtensionContext parent, LauncherStoreFacade launcherStoreFacade,
			NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> closeAction) {
		NamespacedHierarchicalStore<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> parentStore;
		if (parent == null) {
			parentStore = launcherStoreFacade.getRequestLevelStore();
		}
		else {
			parentStore = ((AbstractExtensionContext<?>) parent).valuesStore;
		}
		return new NamespacedHierarchicalStore<>(parentStore, closeAction);
	}

	@Override
	public void close() {
		this.valuesStore.close();
	}

	@Override
	public String getUniqueId() {
		return getTestDescriptor().getUniqueId().toString();
	}

	@Override
	public String getDisplayName() {
		return getTestDescriptor().getDisplayName();
	}

	@Override
	public void publishReportEntry(Map<String, String> values) {
		this.engineExecutionListener.reportingEntryPublished(this.testDescriptor, ReportEntry.from(values));
	}

	@Override
	public void publishFile(String name, MediaType mediaType, ThrowingConsumer<Path> action) {
		Preconditions.notNull(name, "name must not be null");
		Preconditions.notNull(mediaType, "mediaType must not be null");
		Preconditions.notNull(action, "action must not be null");

		publishFileEntry(name, action, file -> {
			Preconditions.condition(Files.isRegularFile(file), () -> "Published path must be a regular file: " + file);
			return FileEntry.from(file, mediaType.toString());
		});
	}

	@Override
	public void publishDirectory(String name, ThrowingConsumer<Path> action) {
		Preconditions.notNull(name, "name must not be null");
		Preconditions.notNull(action, "action must not be null");

		ThrowingConsumer<Path> enhancedAction = path -> {
			if (!Files.isDirectory(path)) {
				Files.createDirectory(path);
			}
			action.accept(path);
		};
		publishFileEntry(name, enhancedAction, file -> {
			Preconditions.condition(Files.isDirectory(file), () -> "Published path must be a directory: " + file);
			return FileEntry.from(file, null);
		});
	}

	private void publishFileEntry(String name, ThrowingConsumer<Path> action,
			Function<Path, FileEntry> fileEntryCreator) {
		Path dir = createOutputDirectory();
		Path path = dir.resolve(name);
		Preconditions.condition(path.getParent() != null && path.getParent().equals(dir),
			() -> "name must not contain path separators: " + name);
		try {
			action.accept(path);
		}
		catch (Throwable t) {
			UnrecoverableExceptions.rethrowIfUnrecoverable(t);
			throw new JUnitException("Failed to publish path", t);
		}
		Preconditions.condition(Files.exists(path), () -> "Published path must exist: " + path);
		FileEntry fileEntry = fileEntryCreator.apply(path);
		this.engineExecutionListener.fileEntryPublished(this.testDescriptor, fileEntry);
	}

	private Path createOutputDirectory() {
		try {
			return configuration.getOutputDirectoryProvider().createOutputDirectory(this.testDescriptor);
		}
		catch (IOException e) {
			throw new JUnitException("Failed to create output directory", e);
		}
	}

	@Override
	public Optional<ExtensionContext> getParent() {
		return Optional.ofNullable(this.parent);
	}

	@Override
	public ExtensionContext getRoot() {
		if (this.parent != null) {
			return this.parent.getRoot();
		}
		return this;
	}

	protected T getTestDescriptor() {
		return this.testDescriptor;
	}

	@Override
	public Store getStore(Namespace namespace) {
		return launcherStoreFacade.getStoreAdapter(this.valuesStore, namespace);
	}

	@Override
	public Store getStore(StoreScope scope, Namespace namespace) {
		return switch (scope) {
			case LAUNCHER_SESSION -> launcherStoreFacade.getSessionLevelStore(namespace);
			case EXECUTION_REQUEST -> launcherStoreFacade.getRequestLevelStore(namespace);
			case EXTENSION_CONTEXT -> getStore(namespace);
		};
	}

	@Override
	public Set<String> getTags() {
		// return modifiable copy
		return new LinkedHashSet<>(this.tags);
	}

	@Override
	public Optional<String> getConfigurationParameter(String key) {
		return this.configuration.getRawConfigurationParameter(key);
	}

	@Override
	public <V> Optional<V> getConfigurationParameter(String key,
			Function<? super String, ? extends @Nullable V> transformer) {
		return this.configuration.getRawConfigurationParameter(key, transformer);
	}

	@Override
	public ExecutionMode getExecutionMode() {
		return toJupiterExecutionMode(getPlatformExecutionMode());
	}

	@Override
	public ExecutableInvoker getExecutableInvoker() {
		return executableInvoker;
	}

	@Override
	public <E extends Extension> List<E> getExtensions(Class<E> extensionType) {
		return extensionRegistry.getExtensions(extensionType);
	}

	protected abstract Node.ExecutionMode getPlatformExecutionMode();

	private ExecutionMode toJupiterExecutionMode(Node.ExecutionMode mode) {
		return switch (mode) {
			case CONCURRENT -> ExecutionMode.CONCURRENT;
			case SAME_THREAD -> ExecutionMode.SAME_THREAD;
		};
	}
}

"""
Simulate the issue where warnings are logged multiple times for the same class type
"""

class CloseableResource:
    """Simulates Store.CloseableResource interface"""
    def close(self):
        pass

class TestCloseableResource(CloseableResource):
    """Simulates a class that implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable"""
    def __init__(self, name):
        self.name = name
    
    def close(self):
        print(f"Closing {self.name}")

def simulate_current_behavior():
    """Simulates current behavior where warning is logged every time"""
    print("=== Current Behavior (logs warning for every instance) ===")
    warned_classes = set()  # Not used in current implementation
    
    for i in range(5):
        resource = TestCloseableResource(f"Resource {i}")
        is_auto_close_enabled = True
        
        # Current implementation (problematic)
        if isinstance(resource, CloseableResource):
            if is_auto_close_enabled:
                # This logs warning every time
                print(f"WARNING: Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: {resource.__class__.__name__}")
            resource.close()

def simulate_fixed_behavior():
    """Simulates fixed behavior where warning is logged only once per class"""
    print("\n=== Fixed Behavior (logs warning once per class) ===")
    warned_classes = set()  # Track which classes we'"'"'ve warned about
    
    for i in range(5):
        resource = TestCloseableResource(f"Resource {i}")
        is_auto_close_enabled = True
        
        # Fixed implementation
        if isinstance(resource, CloseableResource):
            if is_auto_close_enabled:
                class_name = resource.__class__.__name__
                if class_name not in warned_classes:
                    # Only log warning once per class
                    print(f"WARNING: Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: {class_name}")
                    warned_classes.add(class_name)
            resource.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    simulate_current_behavior()
    simulate_fixed_behavior()'

	@SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
	private NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> createCloseAction() {
		return (__, ___, value) -> {
			boolean isAutoCloseEnabled = this.configuration.isClosingStoredAutoCloseablesEnabled();

			if (value instanceof @SuppressWarnings("resource") AutoCloseable closeable && isAutoCloseEnabled) {
				closeable.close();
				return;

			if (value instanceof Store.CloseableResource resource) {
				if (isAutoCloseEnabled) {
					LOGGER.warn(
						() -> "Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: " + value.getClass().getName());
				}
				resource.close();
			}
		};
	}

Now I understand the issue completely. The problem is in the `createCloseAction()` method in `AbstractExtensionContext.java`. Every time a `CloseableResource` instance is closed, it logs a warning, even if multiple instances of the same class type are being closed. This causes spam in the logs.

According to the PR description, we need to log the warning only once per `CloseableResource` implementation class. The solution is to maintain a static set that tracks which classes have already been warned about.

	@SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
	private NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> createCloseAction() {
		return (__, ___, value) -> {
			boolean isAutoCloseEnabled = this.configuration.isClosingStoredAutoCloseablesEnabled();

			if (value instanceof @SuppressWarnings("resource") AutoCloseable closeable && isAutoCloseEnabled) {
				closeable.close();
				return;
			}

			if (value instanceof Store.CloseableResource resource) {
				if (isAutoCloseEnabled) {
					LOGGER.warn(
						() -> "Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: " + value.getClass().getName());
				}
				resource.close();
			}
		};
	}

"""

import re

def fix_abstract_extension_context():

        content = f.read()

            # Insert after the LOGGER field
            insert_pos = match.end()

# Fix for CloseableResource warning spam issue

# Create a temporary file with the fix
cat > /tmp/fix.sed << '"'"'EOF'"'"'
/if (value instanceof Store\.CloseableResource resource) {/,/resource\.close();/c\
		if (value instanceof Store.CloseableResource resource) {\
			if (isAutoCloseEnabled) {\
				String className = value.getClass().getName();\
				if (warnedCloseableResourceClasses.add(className)) {\
					LOGGER.warn(\
						() -> "Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: " + className);\
				}\
			}\
			resource.close();\
		}
EOF

# Apply the fix

echo "Fix applied successfully!"'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/FixCloseableResourceWarning.java --file_text 'import java.io.IOException;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.nio.file.Paths;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.ArrayList;

public class FixCloseableResourceWarning {
    public static void main(String[] args) throws IOException {
        String filePath = "/testbed/junit-jupiter-engine/src/main/java/org/junit/jupiter/engine/descriptor/AbstractExtensionContext.java";
        Path path = Paths.get(filePath);
        
        List<String> lines = Files.readAllLines(path);
        List<String> modifiedLines = new ArrayList<>();
        
        boolean importAdded = false;
        boolean fieldAdded = false;
        boolean warningFixed = false;
        
        for (int i = 0; i < lines.size(); i++) {
            String line = lines.get(i);
            
            // Add import for ConcurrentHashMap after the Set import
            if (!importAdded && line.contains("import java.util.Set;")) {
                modifiedLines.add(line);
                modifiedLines.add("import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;");
                importAdded = true;
                continue;
            }
            
            // Add static field after the LOGGER field
            if (!fieldAdded && line.contains("private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AbstractExtensionContext.class);")) {
                modifiedLines.add(line);
                modifiedLines.add("\tprivate static final Set<String> warnedCloseableResourceClasses = ConcurrentHashMap.newKeySet();");
                fieldAdded = true;
                continue;
            }
            
            // Fix the warning logic
            if (!warningFixed && line.contains("if (value instanceof Store.CloseableResource resource)")) {
                // Start of the CloseableResource block
                modifiedLines.add(line);
                
                // Find the next few lines and modify them
                int j = i + 1;
                while (j < lines.size()) {
                    String nextLine = lines.get(j);
                    
                    if (nextLine.contains("if (isAutoCloseEnabled)")) {
                        modifiedLines.add("\t\t\tif (isAutoCloseEnabled) {");
                        modifiedLines.add("\t\t\t\tString className = value.getClass().getName();");
                        modifiedLines.add("\t\t\t\tif (warnedCloseableResourceClasses.add(className)) {");
                        
                        // Find the LOGGER.warn line
                        j++;
                        while (j < lines.size()) {
                            String warnLine = lines.get(j);
                            if (warnLine.contains("LOGGER.warn")) {
                                // Replace the class name with the variable
                                modifiedLines.add(warnLine.replace("value.getClass().getName()", "className"));
                                break;
                            }
                            j++;
                        }
                        
                        modifiedLines.add("\t\t\t\t}");
                        modifiedLines.add("\t\t\t}");
                        
                        // Skip the original LOGGER.warn and closing brace
                        j++;
                        while (j < lines.size() && !lines.get(j).contains("resource.close()")) {
                            j++;
                        }
                        
                        // Add the resource.close() line
                        if (j < lines.size()) {
                            modifiedLines.add(lines.get(j));
                        }
                        
                        // Add the closing brace
                        j++;
                        if (j < lines.size() && lines.get(j).contains("}")) {
                            modifiedLines.add(lines.get(j));
                        }
                        
                        i = j;
                        warningFixed = true;
                        break;
                    } else {
                        modifiedLines.add(nextLine);
                        j++;
                    }
                }
                
                i = j;
                continue;
            }
            
            modifiedLines.add(line);
        }
        
        // Write the modified content back to the file
        Files.write(path, modifiedLines);
        System.out.println("Fix applied successfully!");
    }
}'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/ManualFix.java --file_text 'import java.io.BufferedReader;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.FileReader;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;

public class ManualFix {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        try {
            String filePath = "/testbed/junit-jupiter-engine/src/main/java/org/junit/jupiter/engine/descriptor/AbstractExtensionContext.java";
            
            // Read the entire file
            StringBuilder content = new StringBuilder();
            try (BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new FileReader(filePath))) {
                String line;
                while ((line = reader.readLine()) != null) {
                    content.append(line).append("\n");
                }
            }
            
            String originalContent = content.toString();
            
            // Step 1: Add import for ConcurrentHashMap
            String importSetLine = "import java.util.Set;";
            String importConcurrentHashMap = "import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;";
            
            if (!originalContent.contains(importConcurrentHashMap)) {
                originalContent = originalContent.replace(importSetLine, importSetLine + "\n" + importConcurrentHashMap);
            }
            
            // Step 2: Add static field after LOGGER declaration
            String loggerField = "private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AbstractExtensionContext.class);";
            String warnedClassesField = "\tprivate static final java.util.Set<String> warnedCloseableResourceClasses = ConcurrentHashMap.newKeySet();";
            
            if (!originalContent.contains("warnedCloseableResourceClasses")) {
                originalContent = originalContent.replace(loggerField, loggerField + "\n" + warnedClassesField);
            }
            
            // Step 3: Replace the warning logic
            String oldWarningSection = """
		if (value instanceof Store.CloseableResource resource) {
			if (isAutoCloseEnabled) {
				LOGGER.warn(
					() -> "Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: " + value.getClass().getName());
			}
			resource.close();
		}""";
            
            String newWarningSection = """
		if (value instanceof Store.CloseableResource resource) {
			if (isAutoCloseEnabled) {
				String className = value.getClass().getName();
				if (warnedCloseableResourceClasses.add(className)) {
					LOGGER.warn(
						() -> "Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: " + className);
				}
			}
			resource.close();
		}""";
            
            originalContent = originalContent.replace(oldWarningSection, newWarningSection);
            
            // Write the modified content back
            try (BufferedWriter writer = new BufferedWriter(new FileWriter(filePath))) {
                writer.write(originalContent);
            }
            
            System.out.println("File modified successfully!");
            
        } catch (IOException e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }
}'

+/*
+ * Copyright 2015-2025 the original author or authors.
+ *
+ * All rights reserved. This program and the accompanying materials are

+package org.junit.jupiter.engine.descriptor;
+
+import static java.util.stream.Collectors.collectingAndThen;
+import static java.util.stream.Collectors.toCollection;
+
+import java.io.IOException;
+import java.nio.file.Files;
+import java.nio.file.Path;
+import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
+import java.util.Collections;
+import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
+import java.util.List;
+import java.util.Map;
+import java.util.Optional;
+import java.util.Set;
+import java.util.function.Function;
+
+import org.jspecify.annotations.Nullable;
+import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExecutableInvoker;
+import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.Extension;
+import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtensionContext;
+import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.MediaType;
+import org.junit.jupiter.api.function.ThrowingConsumer;
+import org.junit.jupiter.api.parallel.ExecutionMode;
+import org.junit.jupiter.engine.config.JupiterConfiguration;
+import org.junit.jupiter.engine.execution.DefaultExecutableInvoker;
+import org.junit.jupiter.engine.extension.ExtensionContextInternal;
+import org.junit.jupiter.engine.extension.ExtensionRegistry;
+import org.junit.platform.commons.JUnitException;
+import org.junit.platform.commons.logging.Logger;
+import org.junit.platform.commons.logging.LoggerFactory;
+import org.junit.platform.commons.util.Preconditions;
+import org.junit.platform.commons.util.UnrecoverableExceptions;
+import org.junit.platform.engine.EngineExecutionListener;
+import org.junit.platform.engine.TestDescriptor;
+import org.junit.platform.engine.TestTag;
+import org.junit.platform.engine.reporting.FileEntry;
+import org.junit.platform.engine.reporting.ReportEntry;
+import org.junit.platform.engine.support.hierarchical.Node;
+import org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.NamespacedHierarchicalStore;
+
+/**
+ * @since 5.0
+ */
+abstract class AbstractExtensionContext<T extends TestDescriptor> implements ExtensionContextInternal, AutoCloseable {
+
+	private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AbstractExtensionContext.class);
+
+	private final @Nullable ExtensionContext parent;
+	private final EngineExecutionListener engineExecutionListener;
+	private final T testDescriptor;
+	private final Set<String> tags;
+private static final Set<String> warnedCloseableResourceClasses = ConcurrentHashMap.newKeySet();
+	private final JupiterConfiguration configuration;
+	private final ExecutableInvoker executableInvoker;
+	private final ExtensionRegistry extensionRegistry;
+	private final LauncherStoreFacade launcherStoreFacade;
+	private final NamespacedHierarchicalStore<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> valuesStore;
+
+	AbstractExtensionContext(@Nullable ExtensionContext parent, EngineExecutionListener engineExecutionListener,
+			T testDescriptor, JupiterConfiguration configuration, ExtensionRegistry extensionRegistry,
+			LauncherStoreFacade launcherStoreFacade) {
+
+		Preconditions.notNull(testDescriptor, "TestDescriptor must not be null");
+		Preconditions.notNull(configuration, "JupiterConfiguration must not be null");
+		Preconditions.notNull(extensionRegistry, "ExtensionRegistry must not be null");
+		this.executableInvoker = new DefaultExecutableInvoker(this, extensionRegistry);
+		this.parent = parent;
+		this.engineExecutionListener = engineExecutionListener;
+		this.testDescriptor = testDescriptor;
+		this.configuration = configuration;
+		this.extensionRegistry = extensionRegistry;
+		this.launcherStoreFacade = launcherStoreFacade;
+
+		// @formatter:off
+		this.tags = testDescriptor.getTags().stream()
+				.map(TestTag::getName)
+				.collect(collectingAndThen(toCollection(LinkedHashSet::new), Collections::unmodifiableSet));
+		// @formatter:on
+
+		this.valuesStore = createStore(parent, launcherStoreFacade, createCloseAction());
+	}
+
+	@SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
+	private NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> createCloseAction() {
+		return (__, ___, value) -> {
+			boolean isAutoCloseEnabled = this.configuration.isClosingStoredAutoCloseablesEnabled();
+
+			if (value instanceof @SuppressWarnings("resource") AutoCloseable closeable && isAutoCloseEnabled) {
+				closeable.close();
+				return;
+			}
+
+			if (value instanceof Store.CloseableResource resource) {
+				if (isAutoCloseEnabled) {
+					LOGGER.warn(
+						() -> "Type implements CloseableResource but not AutoCloseable: " + value.getClass().getName());
+				}
+				resource.close();
+			}
+		};
+	}
+
+	private static NamespacedHierarchicalStore<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> createStore(
+			@Nullable ExtensionContext parent, LauncherStoreFacade launcherStoreFacade,
+			NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> closeAction) {
+		NamespacedHierarchicalStore<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> parentStore;
+		if (parent == null) {
+			parentStore = launcherStoreFacade.getRequestLevelStore();
+		}
+		else {
+			parentStore = ((AbstractExtensionContext<?>) parent).valuesStore;
+		}
+		return new NamespacedHierarchicalStore<>(parentStore, closeAction);
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public void close() {
+		this.valuesStore.close();
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public String getUniqueId() {
+		return getTestDescriptor().getUniqueId().toString();
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public String getDisplayName() {
+		return getTestDescriptor().getDisplayName();
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public void publishReportEntry(Map<String, String> values) {
+		this.engineExecutionListener.reportingEntryPublished(this.testDescriptor, ReportEntry.from(values));
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public void publishFile(String name, MediaType mediaType, ThrowingConsumer<Path> action) {
+		Preconditions.notNull(name, "name must not be null");
+		Preconditions.notNull(mediaType, "mediaType must not be null");
+		Preconditions.notNull(action, "action must not be null");
+
+		publishFileEntry(name, action, file -> {
+			Preconditions.condition(Files.isRegularFile(file), () -> "Published path must be a regular file: " + file);
+			return FileEntry.from(file, mediaType.toString());
+		});
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public void publishDirectory(String name, ThrowingConsumer<Path> action) {
+		Preconditions.notNull(name, "name must not be null");
+		Preconditions.notNull(action, "action must not be null");
+
+		ThrowingConsumer<Path> enhancedAction = path -> {
+			if (!Files.isDirectory(path)) {
+				Files.createDirectory(path);
+			}
+			action.accept(path);
+		};
+		publishFileEntry(name, enhancedAction, file -> {
+			Preconditions.condition(Files.isDirectory(file), () -> "Published path must be a directory: " + file);
+			return FileEntry.from(file, null);
+		});
+	}
+
+	private void publishFileEntry(String name, ThrowingConsumer<Path> action,
+			Function<Path, FileEntry> fileEntryCreator) {
+		Path dir = createOutputDirectory();
+		Path path = dir.resolve(name);
+		Preconditions.condition(path.getParent() != null && path.getParent().equals(dir),
+			() -> "name must not contain path separators: " + name);
+		try {
+			action.accept(path);
+		}
+		catch (Throwable t) {
+			UnrecoverableExceptions.rethrowIfUnrecoverable(t);
+			throw new JUnitException("Failed to publish path", t);
+		}
+		Preconditions.condition(Files.exists(path), () -> "Published path must exist: " + path);
+		FileEntry fileEntry = fileEntryCreator.apply(path);
+		this.engineExecutionListener.fileEntryPublished(this.testDescriptor, fileEntry);
+	}
+
+	private Path createOutputDirectory() {
+		try {
+			return configuration.getOutputDirectoryProvider().createOutputDirectory(this.testDescriptor);
+		}
+		catch (IOException e) {
+			throw new JUnitException("Failed to create output directory", e);
+		}
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public Optional<ExtensionContext> getParent() {
+		return Optional.ofNullable(this.parent);
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public ExtensionContext getRoot() {
+		if (this.parent != null) {
+			return this.parent.getRoot();
+		}
+		return this;
+	}
+
+	protected T getTestDescriptor() {
+		return this.testDescriptor;
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public Store getStore(Namespace namespace) {
+		return launcherStoreFacade.getStoreAdapter(this.valuesStore, namespace);
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public Store getStore(StoreScope scope, Namespace namespace) {
+		return switch (scope) {
+			case LAUNCHER_SESSION -> launcherStoreFacade.getSessionLevelStore(namespace);
+			case EXECUTION_REQUEST -> launcherStoreFacade.getRequestLevelStore(namespace);
+			case EXTENSION_CONTEXT -> getStore(namespace);
+		};
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public Set<String> getTags() {
+		// return modifiable copy
+		return new LinkedHashSet<>(this.tags);
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public Optional<String> getConfigurationParameter(String key) {
+		return this.configuration.getRawConfigurationParameter(key);
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public <V> Optional<V> getConfigurationParameter(String key,
+			Function<? super String, ? extends @Nullable V> transformer) {
+		return this.configuration.getRawConfigurationParameter(key, transformer);
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public ExecutionMode getExecutionMode() {
+		return toJupiterExecutionMode(getPlatformExecutionMode());
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public ExecutableInvoker getExecutableInvoker() {
+		return executableInvoker;
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public <E extends Extension> List<E> getExtensions(Class<E> extensionType) {
+		return extensionRegistry.getExtensions(extensionType);
+	}
+
+	protected abstract Node.ExecutionMode getPlatformExecutionMode();
+
+	private ExecutionMode toJupiterExecutionMode(Node.ExecutionMode mode) {
+		return switch (mode) {
+			case CONCURRENT -> ExecutionMode.CONCURRENT;
+			case SAME_THREAD -> ExecutionMode.SAME_THREAD;
+		};
+	}
+}

+		return (__, ___, value) -> {

+	private static NamespacedHierarchicalStore<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> createStore(
+			@Nullable ExtensionContext parent, LauncherStoreFacade launcherStoreFacade,
+			NamespacedHierarchicalStore.CloseAction<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> closeAction) {
+		NamespacedHierarchicalStore<org.junit.platform.engine.support.store.Namespace> parentStore;
+		if (parent == null) {
+			parentStore = launcherStoreFacade.getRequestLevelStore();
+		}
+		else {

+	@Override
+	public void close() {

+	public String getUniqueId() {

+			Function<Path, FileEntry> fileEntryCreator) {

+		this.engineExecutionListener.fileEntryPublished(this.testDescriptor, fileEntry);
+	}

+	private Path createOutputDirectory() {
+		try {

+		catch (IOException e) {
+			throw new JUnitException("Failed to create output directory", e);
+		}
+	}

+	public ExtensionContext getRoot() {
+		if (this.parent != null) {
+			return this.parent.getRoot();
+		}
+		return this;
+	}
+
+	protected T getTestDescriptor() {
+		return this.testDescriptor;
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public Store getStore(Namespace namespace) {
+		return launcherStoreFacade.getStoreAdapter(this.valuesStore, namespace);
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public Store getStore(StoreScope scope, Namespace namespace) {
+		return switch (scope) {
+			case LAUNCHER_SESSION -> launcherStoreFacade.getSessionLevelStore(namespace);
+			case EXECUTION_REQUEST -> launcherStoreFacade.getRequestLevelStore(namespace);
+			case EXTENSION_CONTEXT -> getStore(namespace);
+		};
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public Set<String> getTags() {
+		// return modifiable copy
+		return new LinkedHashSet<>(this.tags);
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public Optional<String> getConfigurationParameter(String key) {
+		return this.configuration.getRawConfigurationParameter(key);
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public <V> Optional<V> getConfigurationParameter(String key,
+			Function<? super String, ? extends @Nullable V> transformer) {
+		return this.configuration.getRawConfigurationParameter(key, transformer);
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public ExecutionMode getExecutionMode() {
+		return toJupiterExecutionMode(getPlatformExecutionMode());
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public ExecutableInvoker getExecutableInvoker() {
+		return executableInvoker;
+	}
+
+	@Override
+	public <E extends Extension> List<E> getExtensions(Class<E> extensionType) {
+		return extensionRegistry.getExtensions(extensionType);
+	}
+
+	protected abstract Node.ExecutionMode getPlatformExecutionMode();
+
+	private ExecutionMode toJupiterExecutionMode(Node.ExecutionMode mode) {
+		return switch (mode) {
+			case CONCURRENT -> ExecutionMode.CONCURRENT;
+			case SAME_THREAD -> ExecutionMode.SAME_THREAD;
+		};
+	}
+}
